# bullmq - v5.41.8

bullmq - v5.41.8
----------------

  
![](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/95200/143832033-32e868df-f3b0-4251-97fb-c64809a43d36.png)  
  

The fastest, most reliable, Redis-based distributed queue for Node.  
Carefully written for rock solid stability and atomicity.

Read the [documentation](https://docs.bullmq.io)
  
  

 [![](https://img.shields.io/badge/Slack-4A154B)](https://join.slack.com/t/bullmq/shared_invite/zt-1nbtpk6mv-TItWpF9jf3k4yrCaS0PPZA)
[![](https://badge.fury.io/js/bullmq.svg)](https://badge.fury.io/js/bullmq)
[![](https://coveralls.io/repos/github/taskforcesh/bullmq/badge.svg?branch=master)](https://coveralls.io/github/taskforcesh/bullmq?branch=master)
[![](https://img.shields.io/badge/%20%20%F0%9F%93%A6%F0%9F%9A%80-semantic--release-e10079.svg)](https://github.com/semantic-release/semantic-release)
[![](https://img.shields.io/badge/Gurubase-Ask%20BullMQ%20Guru-006BFF)](https://gurubase.io/g/bullmq)

_Follow [@manast](https://twitter.com/manast)
 for \*important\* Bull/BullMQ/BullMQ-Pro news and updates!_

[The gist](#md:the-gist)

=========================

Install:

    $ yarn add bullmq
    

Add jobs to the queue:

    import { Queue } from 'bullmq';const queue = new Queue('Paint');queue.add('cars', { color: 'blue' });
    

Process the jobs in your workers:

    import { Worker } from 'bullmq';const worker = new Worker('Paint', async job => {  if (job.name === 'cars') {    await paintCar(job.data.color);  }});
    

Listen to jobs for completion:

    import { QueueEvents } from 'bullmq';const queueEvents = new QueueEvents('Paint');queueEvents.on('completed', ({ jobId }) => {  console.log('done painting');});queueEvents.on(  'failed',  ({ jobId, failedReason }: { jobId: string; failedReason: string }) => {    console.error('error painting', failedReason);  },);
    

This is just scratching the surface, check all the features and more in the official [documentation](https://docs.bullmq.io)

[Feature Comparison](#md:feature-comparison)

=============================================

Since there are a few job queue solutions, here is a table comparing them:

| Feature | [BullMQ-Pro](https://bullmq.io/#bullmq-pro) | [BullMQ](https://bullmq.io) | Bull | Kue | Bee | Agenda |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Backend | redis | redis | redis | redis | redis | mongo |
| Observables | ✓   |     |     |     |     |     |
| Group Rate Limit | ✓   |     |     |     |     |     |
| Group Support | ✓   |     |     |     |     |     |
| Batches Support | ✓   |     |     |     |     |     |
| Parent/Child Dependencies | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |     |     |
| Debouncing | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |     |
| Priorities | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     | ✓   |
| Concurrency | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| Delayed jobs | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     | ✓   |
| Global events | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |
| Rate Limiter | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |     |
| Pause/Resume | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |
| Sandboxed worker | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |     |
| Repeatable jobs | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |     | ✓   |
| Atomic ops | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     | ✓   |     |
| Persistence | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| UI  | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     | ✓   |
| Optimized for | Jobs / Messages | Jobs / Messages | Jobs / Messages | Jobs | Messages | Jobs |

# AsyncFifoQueue | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [AsyncFifoQueue](v5.AsyncFifoQueue.html)
    

Class AsyncFifoQueue<T>
=======================

AsyncFifoQueue

A minimal FIFO queue for asynchronous operations. Allows adding asynchronous operations and consume them in the order they are resolved.

#### Type Parameters

*   T

# FlowProducer | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [FlowProducer](v5.FlowProducer.html)
    

Class FlowProducer
==================

This class allows to add jobs with dependencies between them in such a way that it is possible to build complex flows. Note: A flow is a tree-like structure of jobs that depend on each other. Whenever the children of a given parent are completed, the parent will be processed, being able to access the children's result data. All Jobs can be in different queues, either children or parents,

#### Hierarchy

*   EventEmitter
    *   FlowProducer

##### Index

### Constructors

[constructor](v5.FlowProducer.html#constructor)

### Properties

[closing](v5.FlowProducer.html#closing)
 [keys](v5.FlowProducer.html#keys)
 [opts](v5.FlowProducer.html#opts)
 [queueKeys](v5.FlowProducer.html#queueKeys)
 [toKey](v5.FlowProducer.html#toKey)

### Accessors

[client](v5.FlowProducer.html#client)

### Methods

[add](v5.FlowProducer.html#add)
 [addBulk](v5.FlowProducer.html#addBulk)
 [close](v5.FlowProducer.html#close)
 [disconnect](v5.FlowProducer.html#disconnect)
 [emit](v5.FlowProducer.html#emit)
 [getFlow](v5.FlowProducer.html#getFlow)
 [off](v5.FlowProducer.html#off)
 [on](v5.FlowProducer.html#on)
 [once](v5.FlowProducer.html#once)
 [waitUntilReady](v5.FlowProducer.html#waitUntilReady)

    \>[](#add.add-1)
    
*   Adds a flow.
    
    This call would be atomic, either it fails and no jobs will be added to the queues, or it succeeds and all jobs will be added.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   flow: [FlowJob](../types/v5.FlowJob.html)
        
        an object with a tree-like structure where children jobs will be processed before their parents.
        
    *   `Optional` opts: [FlowOpts](../interfaces/v5.FlowOpts.html)
        
        options that will be applied to the flow object.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<[JobNode](../interfaces/v5.JobNode.html)
    \>
    

### addBulk[](#addBulk)

*   addBulk(flows): Promise<[JobNode](../interfaces/v5.JobNode.html)
    \[\]\>[](#addBulk.addBulk-1)
    
*   Adds multiple flows.
    
    A flow is a tree-like structure of jobs that depend on each other. Whenever the children of a given parent are completed, the parent will be processed, being able to access the children's result data.
    
    All Jobs can be in different queues, either children or parents, however this call would be atomic, either it fails and no jobs will be added to the queues, or it succeeds and all jobs will be added.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   flows: [FlowJob](../types/v5.FlowJob.html)
        \[\]
        
        an array of objects with a tree-like structure where children jobs will be processed before their parents.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<[JobNode](../interfaces/v5.JobNode.html)
    \[\]\>
    

### close[](#close)

*   close(): Promise<void\>[](#close.close-1)
    
*   Closes the connection and returns a promise that resolves when the connection is closed.
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### disconnect[](#disconnect)

*   disconnect(): Promise<void\>[](#disconnect.disconnect-1)
    
*   Force disconnects a connection.
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>

        \[[U](v5.FlowProducer.html#emit.emit-1.U)\
        \]\>
    
    #### Returns boolean
    

### getFlow[](#getFlow)

    #### Returns Promise<[JobNode](../interfaces/v5.JobNode.html)

RedisJobOptions: [BaseJobOptions](../interfaces/v3.BaseJobOptions.html)
 & {  
    fpof?: boolean;  
    kl?: number;  
}

These fields are the ones stored in Redis with smaller keys for compactness.

#### Type declaration

*   ##### `Optional` fpof?: boolean
    
    If true, moves parent to failed.
    
*   ##### `Optional` kl?: number
    
    Maximum amount of log entries that will be preserved

# Job | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [Job](v5.Job.html)
    

Class Job<DataType, ReturnType, NameType>
=========================================

Job

This class represents a Job in the queue. Normally job are implicitly created when you add a job to the queue with methods such as Queue.addJob( ... )

A Job instance is also passed to the Worker's process function.

Job

#### Type Parameters

*   DataType = any
*   ReturnType = any
*   NameType extends string = string

#### Implements

*   [MinimalJob](../interfaces/v5.MinimalJob.html)

    , [ReturnType](v5.Job.html#constructor.new_Job.ReturnType-1)
    , [NameType](v5.Job.html#constructor.new_Job.NameType-1)
    \>

Properties
----------

### attemptsMade[](#attemptsMade)

attemptsMade: number = 0

Number of attempts after the job has failed.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### attemptsStarted[](#attemptsStarted)

attemptsStarted: number = 0

Number of attempts when job is moved to active.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### data[](#data)

data: [DataType](v5.Job.html#constructor.new_Job.DataType-1)

The payload for this job.

### `Optional` debounceId[](#debounceId)

debounceId?: string

Debounce identifier.

#### Deprecated

use deduplicationId

### `Optional` deduplicationId[](#deduplicationId)

deduplicationId?: string

Deduplication identifier.

### delay[](#delay)

delay: number = 0

An amount of milliseconds to wait until this job can be processed.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### failedReason[](#failedReason)

failedReason: string

Reason for failing.

### `Optional` finishedOn[](#finishedOn)

finishedOn?: number

Timestamp for when the job finished (completed or failed).

### `Optional` id[](#id)

id?: string

### name[](#name)

name: [NameType](v5.Job.html#constructor.new_Job.NameType-1)

The name of the Job

### `Optional` nextRepeatableJobId[](#nextRepeatableJobId)

nextRepeatableJobId?: string

Produced next repetable job Id.

### opts[](#opts)

opts: [JobsOptions](../types/v5.JobsOptions.html)
 = {}

The options object for this job.

### `Optional` parent[](#parent)

parent?: [ParentKeys](../interfaces/v5.ParentKeys.html)

Object that contains parentId (id) and parent queueKey.

### `Optional` parentKey[](#parentKey)

parentKey?: string

Fully qualified key (including the queue prefix) pointing to the parent of this job.

### priority[](#priority)

priority: number = 0

Ranges from 0 (highest priority) to 2 097 152 (lowest priority). Note that using priorities has a slight impact on performance, so do not use it if not required.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` processedBy[](#processedBy)

processedBy?: string

The worker name that is processing or processed this job.

### `Optional` processedOn[](#processedOn)

processedOn?: number

Timestamp for when the job was processed.

### progress[](#progress)

progress: number | object = 0

The progress a job has performed so far.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Readonly` queueQualifiedName[](#queueQualifiedName)

queueQualifiedName: string

It includes the prefix, the namespace separator :, and queue name.

#### See

[https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html\_node/Qualified-Names.html](https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html_node/Qualified-Names.html)

### `Optional` repeatJobKey[](#repeatJobKey)

repeatJobKey?: string

Base repeat job key.

### returnvalue[](#returnvalue)

returnvalue: [ReturnType](v5.Job.html#constructor.new_Job.ReturnType-1)
 = null

The value returned by the processor when processing this job.

#### Default Value

    null
    

### stacktrace[](#stacktrace)

stacktrace: string\[\] = null

Stacktrace for the error (for failed jobs).

#### Default Value

    null
    

### timestamp[](#timestamp)

timestamp: number

Timestamp when the job was created (unless overridden with job options).

### `Optional` token[](#token)

token?: string

The token used for locking this job.

### getDependencies[](#getDependencies)

*   getDependencies(opts?): Promise<{  
        nextProcessedCursor?: number;  
        nextUnprocessedCursor?: number;  
        processed?: Record<string, any\>;  
        unprocessed?: string\[\];  
    }\>[](#getDependencies.getDependencies-1)
    
*   Get children job keys if this job is a parent and has children.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   opts: [DependenciesOpts](../interfaces/v5.DependenciesOpts.html)
         = {}
    
    #### Returns Promise<{  
        nextProcessedCursor?: number;  
        nextUnprocessedCursor?: number;  
        processed?: Record<string, any\>;  
        unprocessed?: string\[\];  
    }\>
    
    dependencies separated by processed and unprocessed.
    
    #### Remarks
    
    Count options before Redis v7.2 works as expected with any quantity of entries on processed/unprocessed dependencies, since v7.2 you must consider that count won't have any effect until processed/unprocessed dependencies have a length greater than 127
    
    #### See
    
    [https://redis.io/docs/management/optimization/memory-optimization/#redis--72](https://redis.io/docs/management/optimization/memory-optimization/#redis--72)

        *   ##### `Optional` processed?: boolean

    #### Returns Promise<{  
        processed?: number;  
        unprocessed?: number;  
    }\>
    
    dependencies count separated by processed and unprocessed.

    \>

### retry[](#retry)

*   retry(state?): Promise<void\>[](#retry.retry-1)
    
*   Attempts to retry the job. Only a job that has failed or completed can be retried.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   state: [FinishedStatus](../types/v5.FinishedStatus.html)
         = 'failed'
        
        completed / failed
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    
    If resolved and return code is 1, then the queue emits a waiting event otherwise the operation was not a success and throw the corresponding error. If the promise rejects, it indicates that the script failed to execute

# JobScheduler | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [JobScheduler](v5.JobScheduler.html)
    

Class JobScheduler
==================

QueueBase

#### Description

Base class for all classes that need to interact with queues. This class is normally not used directly, but extended by the other classes.

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.JobScheduler)
)

*   [QueueBase](v5.QueueBase.html)
    *   JobScheduler

# Queue | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [Queue](v5.Queue.html)
    

Class Queue<DataTypeOrJob, DefaultResultType, DefaultNameType, DataType, ResultType, NameType>
==============================================================================================

Queue

This class provides methods to add jobs to a queue and some other high-level administration such as pausing or deleting queues.

#### Example

    import { Queue } from 'bullmq';interface MyDataType { foo: string;}interface MyResultType {  bar: string;}const queue = new Queue<MyDataType, MyResultType, "blue" | "brown">('myQueue');
    

#### Type Parameters

*   DataTypeOrJob = any
*   DefaultResultType = any
*   DefaultNameType extends string = string
*   DataType = ExtractDataType<[DataTypeOrJob](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataTypeOrJob-1)
    , [DataTypeOrJob](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataTypeOrJob-1)
    \>
    
    The type of the data that the job will process.
    
*   ResultType = ExtractResultType<[DataTypeOrJob](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataTypeOrJob-1)
    , [DefaultResultType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DefaultResultType-1)
    \>
    
    The type of the result of the job.
    
*   NameType extends string = ExtractNameType<[DataTypeOrJob](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataTypeOrJob-1)
    , [DefaultNameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DefaultNameType-1)
    \>
    
    The type of the name of the job.

*   Adds a new job to the queue.

### addBulk[](#addBulk)

*   addBulk(jobs): Promise<[Job](v5.Job.html)
    <[DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
    , [ResultType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.ResultType-1)
    , [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
    \>\[\]\>[](#addBulk.addBulk-1)
    
*   Adds an array of jobs to the queue. This method may be faster than adding one job at a time in a sequence.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobs: {  
            data: [DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
        ;  
            name: [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
        ;  
            opts?: [BulkJobOptions](../types/v5.BulkJobOptions.html)
        ;  
        }\[\]
        
        The array of jobs to add to the queue. Each job is defined by 3 properties, 'name', 'data' and 'opts'. They follow the same signature as 'Queue.add'.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<[Job](v5.Job.html)
    <[DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
    , [ResultType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.ResultType-1)
    , [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
    \>\[\]\>
    

### addJobLog[](#addJobLog)

*   addJobLog(jobId, logRow, keepLogs?): Promise<number\>[](#addJobLog.addJobLog-1)
    
*   Logs one row of job's log data.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobId: string
        
        The job id to log against.
        
    *   logRow: string
        
        String with log data to be logged.
        
    *   `Optional` keepLogs: number
        
        Max number of log entries to keep (0 for unlimited).
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<number\>
    
    The total number of log entries for this job so far.
    

### clean[](#clean)

*   clean(grace, limit, type?): Promise<string\[\]\>[](#clean.clean-1)
    
*   Cleans jobs from a queue. Similar to drain but keeps jobs within a certain grace period.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   grace: number
        
        The grace period in milliseconds
        
    *   limit: number
        
        Max number of jobs to clean
        
    *   type: "failed" | "active" | "paused" | "completed" | "wait" | "prioritized" | "delayed" = 'completed'
        
        The type of job to clean Possible values are completed, wait, active, paused, delayed, failed. Defaults to completed.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<string\[\]\>
    
    Id jobs from the deleted records

### drain[](#drain)

*   drain(delayed?): Promise<void\>[](#drain.drain-1)
    
*   Drains the queue, i.e., removes all jobs that are waiting or delayed, but not active, completed or failed.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   delayed: boolean = false
        
        Pass true if it should also clean the delayed jobs.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>

### getDependencies[](#getDependencies)

*   getDependencies(parentId, type, start, end): Promise<{  
        items: {  
            err?: string;  
            id: string;  
            v?: any;  
        }\[\];  
        jobs: [JobJsonRaw](../interfaces/v5.JobJsonRaw.html)
    \[\];  
        total: number;  
    }\>[](#getDependencies.getDependencies-1)
    
*   Returns the qualified job ids and the raw job data (if available) of the children jobs of the given parent job. It is possible to get either the already processed children, in this case an array of qualified job ids and their result values will be returned, or the pending children, in this case an array of qualified job ids will be returned. A qualified job id is a string representing the job id in a given queue, for example: "bull:myqueue:jobid".
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   parentId: string
        
        The id of the parent job
        
    *   type: "pending" | "processed"
        
        "processed" | "pending"
        
    *   start: number
    *   end: number
    
    #### Returns Promise<{  
        items: {  
            err?: string;  
            id: string;  
            v?: any;  
        }\[\];  
        jobs: [JobJsonRaw](../interfaces/v5.JobJsonRaw.html)
    \[\];  
        total: number;  
    }\>

### getMetrics[](#getMetrics)

*   getMetrics(type, start?, end?): Promise<[Metrics](../interfaces/v5.Metrics.html)
    \>[](#getMetrics.getMetrics-1)
    
*   Get queue metrics related to the queue.
    
    This method returns the gathered metrics for the queue. The metrics are represented as an array of job counts per unit of time (1 minute).
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   type: "failed" | "completed"
    *   start: number = 0
        
        Start point of the metrics, where 0 is the newest point to be returned.
        
    *   end: number = -1
        
        End point of the metrics, where -1 is the oldest point to be returned.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<[Metrics](../interfaces/v5.Metrics.html)
    \>
    
    *   Returns an object with queue metrics.

### obliterate[](#obliterate)

*   obliterate(opts?): Promise<void\>[](#obliterate.obliterate-1)
    
*   Completely destroys the queue and all of its contents irreversibly. This method will the _pause_ the queue and requires that there are no active jobs. It is possible to bypass this requirement, i.e. not having active jobs using the "force" option.
    
    Note: This operation requires to iterate on all the jobs stored in the queue and can be slow for very large queues.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Optional` opts: [ObliterateOpts](../interfaces/v5.ObliterateOpts.html)
        
        Obliterate options.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>

### pause[](#pause)

*   pause(): Promise<void\>[](#pause.pause-1)
    
*   Pauses the processing of this queue globally.
    
    We use an atomic RENAME operation on the wait queue. Since we have blocking calls with BRPOPLPUSH on the wait queue, as long as the queue is renamed to 'paused', no new jobs will be processed (the current ones will run until finalized).
    
    Adding jobs requires a LUA script to check first if the paused list exist and in that case it will add it there instead of the wait list.
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### promoteJobs[](#promoteJobs)

*   promoteJobs(opts?): Promise<void\>[](#promoteJobs.promoteJobs-1)
    
*   Promote all the delayed jobs.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   opts: {  
            count?: number;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional` count?: number
            
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### rateLimit[](#rateLimit)

*   remove(jobId, opts?): Promise<number\>[](#remove.remove-1)
    
*   Removes the given job from the queue as well as all its dependencies.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobId: string
        
        The id of the job to remove
        
    *   opts: {  
            removeChildren: boolean;  
        } = {}
        
        Options to remove a job
        
        *   ##### removeChildren: boolean
            
    
    #### Returns Promise<number\>
    
    1 if it managed to remove the job or 0 if the job or any of its dependencies were locked.

### removeRepeatableByKey[](#removeRepeatableByKey)

*   removeRepeatableByKey(key): Promise<boolean\>[](#removeRepeatableByKey.removeRepeatableByKey-1)
    
*   Removes a repeatable job by its key. Note that the key is the one used to store the repeatable job metadata and not one of the job iterations themselves. You can use "getRepeatableJobs" in order to get the keys.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   key: string
    
    #### Returns Promise<boolean\>
    
    #### See

    #### Deprecated

### setGlobalConcurrency[](#setGlobalConcurrency)

*   setGlobalConcurrency(concurrency): Promise<number\>[](#setGlobalConcurrency.setGlobalConcurrency-1)
    
*   Enable and set global concurrency value.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   concurrency: number
        
        Maximum number of simultaneous jobs that the workers can handle. For instance, setting this value to 1 ensures that no more than one job is processed at any given time. If this limit is not defined, there will be no restriction on the number of concurrent jobs.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<number\>

### upsertJobScheduler[](#upsertJobScheduler)

*   upsertJobScheduler(jobSchedulerId, repeatOpts, jobTemplate?): Promise<[Job](v5.Job.html)
    <[DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
    , [ResultType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.ResultType-1)
    , [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
    \>\>[](#upsertJobScheduler.upsertJobScheduler-1)
    
*   Upserts a scheduler.
    
    A scheduler is a job factory that creates jobs at a given interval. Upserting a scheduler will create a new job scheduler or update an existing one. It will also create the first job based on the repeat options and delayed accordingly.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobSchedulerId: [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
        
    *   repeatOpts: Omit<[RepeatOptions](../interfaces/v5.RepeatOptions.html)
        , "key"\>
        
        Repeat options
        
    *   `Optional` jobTemplate: {  
            data?: [DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
        ;  
            name?: [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
        ;  
            opts?: [JobSchedulerTemplateOptions](../types/v5.JobSchedulerTemplateOptions.html)
        ;  
        }
        
        Job template. If provided it will be used for all the jobs created by the scheduler.
        
        *   ##### `Optional` data?: [DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
            
        *   ##### `Optional` name?: [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
            
        *   ##### `Optional` opts?: [JobSchedulerTemplateOptions](../types/v5.JobSchedulerTemplateOptions.html)
            
    
    #### Returns Promise<[Job](v5.Job.html)
    <[DataType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.DataType-1)
    , [ResultType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.ResultType-1)
    , [NameType](v5.Queue.html#constructor.new_Queue.NameType-1)
    \>\>
    
    The next job to be scheduled (would normally be in delayed state).

Class QueueGetters<JobBase>
===========================

QueueGetters

            v?: any;  
        }\[\];  
        jobs: [JobJsonRaw](../interfaces/v5.JobJsonRaw.html)
    \[\];  
        total: number;  
    }\>[](#getDependencies.getDependencies-1)
    
*   Returns the qualified job ids and the raw job data (if available) of the children jobs of the given parent job. It is possible to get either the already processed children, in this case an array of qualified job ids and their result values will be returned, or the pending children, in this case an array of qualified job ids will be returned. A qualified job id is a string representing the job id in a given queue, for example: "bull:myqueue:jobid".
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   parentId: string
        
        The id of the parent job
        
    *   type: "pending" | "processed"
        
        "processed" | "pending"
        
    *   start: number
    *   end: number
    
    #### Returns Promise<{  
        items: {  
            err?: string;  
            id: string;  
            v?: any;  
        }\[\];  
        jobs: [JobJsonRaw](../interfaces/v5.JobJsonRaw.html)
    \[\];  
        total: number;  
    }\>

### getJobCountByTypes[](#getJobCountByTypes)

*   getJobCountByTypes(...types): Promise<number\>[](#getJobCountByTypes.getJobCountByTypes-1)
    
*   Job counts by type
    
    Queue#getJobCountByTypes('completed') => completed count Queue#getJobCountByTypes('completed,failed') => completed + failed count Queue#getJobCountByTypes('completed', 'failed') => completed + failed count Queue#getJobCountByTypes('completed', 'waiting', 'failed') => completed + waiting + failed count
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Rest` ...types: [JobType](../types/v5.JobType.html)
        \[\]
    
    #### Returns Promise<number\>

### getMetrics[](#getMetrics)

*   getMetrics(type, start?, end?): Promise<[Metrics](../interfaces/v5.Metrics.html)
    \>[](#getMetrics.getMetrics-1)
    
*   Get queue metrics related to the queue.
    
    This method returns the gathered metrics for the queue. The metrics are represented as an array of job counts per unit of time (1 minute).
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   type: "failed" | "completed"
    *   start: number = 0
        
        Start point of the metrics, where 0 is the newest point to be returned.
        
    *   end: number = -1
        
        End point of the metrics, where -1 is the oldest point to be returned.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<[Metrics](../interfaces/v5.Metrics.html)
    \>
    
    *   Returns an object with queue metrics.

### getRateLimitTtl[](#getRateLimitTtl)

*   getRateLimitTtl(maxJobs?): Promise<number\>[](#getRateLimitTtl.getRateLimitTtl-1)
    
*   Returns the time to live for a rate limited key in milliseconds.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Optional` maxJobs: number
        
        max jobs to be considered in rate limit state. If not passed it will return the remaining ttl without considering if max jobs is excedeed.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<number\>
    
    \-2 if the key does not exist. -1 if the key exists but has no associated expire.
    
    #### See
    
    [https://redis.io/commands/pttl/](https://redis.io/commands/pttl/)

# QueueBase | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [QueueBase](v5.QueueBase.html)
    

Class QueueBase
===============

QueueBase

#### Description

Base class for all classes that need to interact with queues. This class is normally not used directly, but extended by the other classes.

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.QueueBase)
)

*   EventEmitter
    *   QueueBase
        *   [JobScheduler](v5.JobScheduler.html)
            
        *   [QueueEvents](v5.QueueEvents.html)
            
        *   [QueueEventsProducer](v5.QueueEventsProducer.html)
            
        *   [QueueGetters](v5.QueueGetters.html)
            
        *   [Repeat](v5.Repeat.html)
            
        *   [Worker](v5.Worker.html)
            

#### Implements

*   [MinimalQueue](../types/v5.MinimalQueue.html)
    

##### Index

### Constructors

[constructor](v5.QueueBase.html#constructor)

### Properties

 [keys](v5.QueueBase.html#keys)
 [name](v5.QueueBase.html#name)
 [opts](v5.QueueBase.html#opts)
 [qualifiedName](v5.QueueBase.html#qualifiedName)
 [toKey](v5.QueueBase.html#toKey)

# QueueEvents | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [QueueEvents](v5.QueueEvents.html)
    

Class QueueEvents
=================

The QueueEvents class is used for listening to the global events emitted by a given queue.

This class requires a dedicated redis connection.

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.QueueEvents)
)

*   [QueueBase](v5.QueueBase.html)
    *   QueueEvents

# Repeat | bullmq - v5.41.8

Class Repeat
============

QueueBase

#### Description

Base class for all classes that need to interact with queues. This class is normally not used directly, but extended by the other classes.

# Worker | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [Worker](v5.Worker.html)
    

Class Worker<DataType, ResultType, NameType>
============================================

This class represents a worker that is able to process jobs from the queue. As soon as the class is instantiated and a connection to Redis is established it will start processing jobs.

#### Type Parameters

*   DataType = any
*   ResultType = any
*   NameType extends string = string

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.Worker)
)

*   [QueueBase](v5.QueueBase.html)
    *   Worker

##### Index

Methods
-------

### close[](#close)

*   close(force?): Promise<void\>[](#close.close-1)
    
*   Closes the worker and related redis connections.
    
    This method waits for current jobs to finalize before returning.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   force: boolean = false
        
        Use force boolean parameter if you do not want to wait for current jobs to be processed. When using telemetry, be mindful that it can interfere with the proper closure of spans, potentially preventing them from being exported.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    
    Promise that resolves when the worker has been closed.
    

### delay[](#delay)

*   delay(milliseconds?, abortController?): Promise<void\>[](#delay.delay-1)
    
*   This function is exposed only for testing purposes.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Optional` milliseconds: number
    *   `Optional` abortController: AbortController
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### disconnect[](#disconnect)

    #### Returns Promise<void\>

*   #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### startStalledCheckTimer[](#startStalledCheckTimer)

*   startStalledCheckTimer(): Promise<void\>[](#startStalledCheckTimer.startStalledCheckTimer-1)
    
*   Manually starts the stalled checker. The check will run once as soon as this method is called, and then every opts.stalledInterval milliseconds until the worker is closed. Note: Normally you do not need to call this method, since the stalled checker is automatically started when the worker starts processing jobs after calling run. However if you want to process the jobs manually you need to call this method to start the stalled checker.
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    
    #### See
    
    [https://docs.bullmq.io/patterns/manually-fetching-jobs](https://docs.bullmq.io/patterns/manually-fetching-jobs)
    

### trace[](#trace)

*   trace<[T](v5.Worker.html#trace.trace-1.T)
    \>(spanKind, operation, destination, callback, srcPropagationMetadata?): Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
     | Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
    \>\>[](#trace.trace-1)
    
*   Wraps the code with telemetry and provides a span for configuration.
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   T
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   spanKind: [SpanKind](../enums/v5.SpanKind.html)
        
        kind of the span: Producer, Consumer, Internal
        
    *   operation: string
        
        operation name (such as add, process, etc)
        
    *   destination: string
        
        destination name (normally the queue name)
        
    *   callback: ((span?, dstPropagationMetadata?) => [T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
         | Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
        \>)
        
        code to wrap with telemetry
        
        *   *   (span?, dstPropagationMetadata?): [T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
                 | Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
                \>
            *   #### Parameters
                
                *   `Optional` span: [Span](../interfaces/v5.Span.html)
                    <any\>
                *   `Optional` dstPropagationMetadata: string
                
                #### Returns [T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
                 | Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
                \>
                
    *   `Optional` srcPropagationMetadata: string
    
    #### Returns Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
     | Promise<[T](v5.JobScheduler.html#trace.trace-1.T)
    \>\>

### moveJobFromActiveToWait[](#moveJobFromActiveToWait)

*   moveJobFromActiveToWait(jobId, token): Promise<any\>[](#moveJobFromActiveToWait.moveJobFromActiveToWait-1)
    
*   Moves a job back from Active to Wait. This script is used when a job has been manually rate limited and needs to be moved back to wait from active status.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobId: string
        
        Job id
        
    *   token: string
    
    #### Returns Promise<any\>
    

### moveStalledJobsToWait[](#moveStalledJobsToWait)

*   moveStalledJobsToWait(): Promise<\[string\[\], string\[\]\]\>[](#moveStalledJobsToWait.moveStalledJobsToWait-1)
    
*   Looks for unlocked jobs in the active queue.
    
    The job was being worked on, but the worker process died and it failed to renew the lock. We call these jobs 'stalled'. This is the most common case. We resolve these by moving them back to wait to be re-processed. To prevent jobs from cycling endlessly between active and wait, (e.g. if the job handler keeps crashing), we limit the number stalled job recoveries to settings.maxStalledCount.
    
    #### Returns Promise<\[string\[\], string\[\]\]\>

### moveToWaitingChildren[](#moveToWaitingChildren)

*   moveToWaitingChildren(jobId, token, opts?): Promise<boolean\>[](#moveToWaitingChildren.moveToWaitingChildren-1)
    
*   Move parent job to waiting-children state.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   jobId: string
    *   token: string
    *   opts: [MoveToWaitingChildrenOpts](../interfaces/v5.MoveToWaitingChildrenOpts.html)
         = {}
    
    #### Returns Promise<boolean\>
    
    true if job is successfully moved, false if there are pending dependencies.
    
    #### Throws
    
    JobNotExist This exception is thrown if jobId is missing.
    
    #### Throws
    
    JobLockNotExist This exception is thrown if job lock is missing.
    
    #### Throws
    
    JobNotInState This exception is thrown if job is not in active state.

### reprocessJob[](#reprocessJob)

*   reprocessJob<[T](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.T-2)
    , [R](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.R-2)
    , [N](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.N-2)
    \>(job, state): Promise<void\>[](#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1)
    
*   Attempts to reprocess a job
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   T = any
    *   R = any
    *   N extends string = string
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   job: [MinimalJob](../interfaces/v5.MinimalJob.html)
        <[T](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.T-2)
        , [R](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.R-2)
        , [N](v5.Scripts.html#reprocessJob.reprocessJob-1.N-2)
        \>
    *   state: "failed" | "completed"
        
        The expected job state. If the job is not found on the provided state, then it's not reprocessed. Supported states: 'failed', 'completed'
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    
    Returns a promise that evaluates to a return code: 1 means the operation was a success 0 means the job does not exist -1 means the job is currently locked and can't be retried. -2 means the job was not found in the expected set

# BaseJobOptions | bullmq - v5.41.8

Interface BaseJobOptions
========================

interface BaseJobOptions {  
    [attempts](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#attempts)
?: number;  
    [backoff](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#backoff)
?: number | [BackoffOptions](v5.BackoffOptions.html)
;  
    [delay](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#delay)
?: number;  
    [jobId](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#jobId)
?: string;  
    [keepLogs](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#keepLogs)
?: number;  
    [lifo](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#lifo)
?: boolean;  
    [parent](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#parent)
?: {  
        id: string;  
        queue: string;  
    };  
    [prevMillis](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#prevMillis)
?: number;  
    [priority](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#priority)
?: number;  
    [removeOnComplete](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#removeOnComplete)
?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)
;  
    [removeOnFail](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#removeOnFail)
?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)
;  
    [repeat](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#repeat)
?: [RepeatOptions](v5.RepeatOptions.html)
;  
    [repeatJobKey](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#repeatJobKey)
?: string;  
    [sizeLimit](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#sizeLimit)
?: number;  
    [stackTraceLimit](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#stackTraceLimit)
?: number;  
    [timestamp](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#timestamp)
?: number;  
}

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.BaseJobOptions)
)

*   [DefaultJobOptions](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html)
    *   BaseJobOptions

##### Index

### Properties

[attempts?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#attempts)
 [backoff?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#backoff)
 [delay?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#delay)
 [jobId?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#jobId)
 [keepLogs?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#keepLogs)
 [lifo?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#lifo)
 [parent?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#parent)
 [prevMillis?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#prevMillis)
 [priority?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#priority)
 [removeOnComplete?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#removeOnComplete)
 [removeOnFail?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#removeOnFail)
 [repeat?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#repeat)
 [repeatJobKey?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#repeatJobKey)
 [sizeLimit?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#sizeLimit)
 [stackTraceLimit?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#stackTraceLimit)
 [timestamp?](v5.BaseJobOptions.html#timestamp)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` attempts[](#attempts)

attempts?: number

The total number of attempts to try the job until it completes.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` backoff[](#backoff)

backoff?: number | [BackoffOptions](v5.BackoffOptions.html)

Backoff setting for automatic retries if the job fails

### `Optional` delay[](#delay)

delay?: number

An amount of milliseconds to wait until this job can be processed. Note that for accurate delays, worker and producers should have their clocks synchronized.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` jobId[](#jobId)

jobId?: string

Override the job ID - by default, the job ID is a unique integer, but you can use this setting to override it. If you use this option, it is up to you to ensure the jobId is unique. If you attempt to add a job with an id that already exists, it will not be added.

### `Optional` keepLogs[](#keepLogs)

keepLogs?: number

Maximum amount of log entries that will be preserved

### `Optional` lifo[](#lifo)

lifo?: boolean

If true, adds the job to the right of the queue instead of the left (default false)

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/lifo](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/lifo)

### `Optional` parent[](#parent)

parent?: {  
    id: string;  
    queue: string;  
}

#### Type declaration

*   ##### id: string
    
*   ##### queue: string
    
    It includes the prefix, the namespace separator :, and queue name.
    
    #### See
    
    [https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html\_node/Qualified-Names.html](https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html_node/Qualified-Names.html)
    

### `Optional` prevMillis[](#prevMillis)

prevMillis?: number

Internal property used by repeatable jobs.

### `Optional` priority[](#priority)

priority?: number

Ranges from 0 (highest priority) to 2 097 152 (lowest priority). Note that using priorities has a slight impact on performance, so do not use it if not required.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` removeOnComplete[](#removeOnComplete)

removeOnComplete?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

If true, removes the job when it successfully completes When given a number, it specifies the maximum amount of jobs to keep, or you can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. It overrides whatever setting is used in the worker. Default behavior is to keep the job in the completed set.

### `Optional` removeOnFail[](#removeOnFail)

removeOnFail?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

If true, removes the job when it fails after all attempts. When given a number, it specifies the maximum amount of jobs to keep, or you can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. It overrides whatever setting is used in the worker. Default behavior is to keep the job in the failed set.

### `Optional` repeat[](#repeat)

repeat?: [RepeatOptions](v5.RepeatOptions.html)

Repeat this job, for example based on a `cron` schedule.

### `Optional` repeatJobKey[](#repeatJobKey)

repeatJobKey?: string

Internal property used by repeatable jobs to save base repeat job key.

### `Optional` sizeLimit[](#sizeLimit)

sizeLimit?: number

Limits the size in bytes of the job's data payload (as a JSON serialized string).

### `Optional` stackTraceLimit[](#stackTraceLimit)

stackTraceLimit?: number

Limits the amount of stack trace lines that will be recorded in the stacktrace.

### `Optional` timestamp[](#timestamp)

timestamp?: number

Timestamp when the job was created.

#### Default Value

    Date.now()
    

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

### On This Page

*   [attempts](#attempts)
    
*   [backoff](#backoff)
    
*   [delay](#delay)
    
*   [jobId](#jobId)
    
*   [keepLogs](#keepLogs)
    
*   [lifo](#lifo)
    
*   [parent](#parent)
    
*   [prevMillis](#prevMillis)
    
*   [priority](#priority)
    
*   [removeOnComplete](#removeOnComplete)

*   [repeat](#repeat)

*   [sizeLimit](#sizeLimit)
    
*   [stackTraceLimit](#stackTraceLimit)
    
*   [timestamp](#timestamp)

Interface ContextManager<Context>
=================================

Context manager interface

The context manager is responsible for managing the context and propagating it across the application.

interface ContextManager<[Context](v5.ContextManager.html#Context)
\> {  
    [active](v5.ContextManager.html#active.active-1)
(): [Context](v5.ContextManager.html#Context)
;

(activeContext, metadata): [Context](v5.ContextManager.html#Context)
;  
    [getMetadata](v5.ContextManager.html#getMetadata.getMetadata-1)
(context): string;  
    [with](v5.ContextManager.html#with.with-1)
<[A](v5.ContextManager.html#with.with-1.A)
\>(context, fn): ReturnType<[A](v5.ContextManager.html#with.with-1.A)
\>;

?: number | [BackoffOptions](v5.BackoffOptions.html)
;  
    [delay](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#delay)
?: number;  
    [keepLogs](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#keepLogs)
?: number;  
    [lifo](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#lifo)
?: boolean;  
    [priority](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#priority)
?: number;  
    [removeOnComplete](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#removeOnComplete)
?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)
;  
    [removeOnFail](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#removeOnFail)
?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)
;  
    [sizeLimit](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#sizeLimit)
?: number;  
    [stackTraceLimit](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#stackTraceLimit)
?: number;  
    [timestamp](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#timestamp)
?: number;  
}

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.DefaultJobOptions)
)

*   DefaultJobOptions
    *   [BaseJobOptions](v5.BaseJobOptions.html)
        

##### Index

### Properties

[attempts?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#attempts)
 [backoff?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#backoff)
 [delay?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#delay)
 [keepLogs?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#keepLogs)
 [lifo?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#lifo)
 [priority?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#priority)
 [removeOnComplete?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#removeOnComplete)
 [removeOnFail?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#removeOnFail)
 [sizeLimit?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#sizeLimit)
 [stackTraceLimit?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#stackTraceLimit)
 [timestamp?](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html#timestamp)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` attempts[](#attempts)

attempts?: number

The total number of attempts to try the job until it completes.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` backoff[](#backoff)

backoff?: number | [BackoffOptions](v5.BackoffOptions.html)

Backoff setting for automatic retries if the job fails

### `Optional` delay[](#delay)

delay?: number

An amount of milliseconds to wait until this job can be processed. Note that for accurate delays, worker and producers should have their clocks synchronized.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` keepLogs[](#keepLogs)

keepLogs?: number

Maximum amount of log entries that will be preserved

### `Optional` lifo[](#lifo)

lifo?: boolean

If true, adds the job to the right of the queue instead of the left (default false)

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/lifo](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/lifo)

### `Optional` priority[](#priority)

priority?: number

Ranges from 0 (highest priority) to 2 097 152 (lowest priority). Note that using priorities has a slight impact on performance, so do not use it if not required.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` removeOnComplete[](#removeOnComplete)

removeOnComplete?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

If true, removes the job when it successfully completes When given a number, it specifies the maximum amount of jobs to keep, or you can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. It overrides whatever setting is used in the worker. Default behavior is to keep the job in the completed set.

### `Optional` removeOnFail[](#removeOnFail)

removeOnFail?: number | boolean | [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

If true, removes the job when it fails after all attempts. When given a number, it specifies the maximum amount of jobs to keep, or you can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. It overrides whatever setting is used in the worker. Default behavior is to keep the job in the failed set.

### `Optional` sizeLimit[](#sizeLimit)

sizeLimit?: number

Limits the size in bytes of the job's data payload (as a JSON serialized string).

### `Optional` stackTraceLimit[](#stackTraceLimit)

stackTraceLimit?: number

Limits the amount of stack trace lines that will be recorded in the stacktrace.

### `Optional` timestamp[](#timestamp)

timestamp?: number

Timestamp when the job was created.

#### Default Value

    Date.now()
    

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

### On This Page

*   [attempts](#attempts)
    
*   [backoff](#backoff)
    
*   [delay](#delay)
    
*   [keepLogs](#keepLogs)
    
*   [lifo](#lifo)
    
*   [priority](#priority)
    
*   [removeOnComplete](#removeOnComplete)
    
*   [removeOnFail](#removeOnFail)
    
*   [sizeLimit](#sizeLimit)

Interface KeepJobs
==================

KeepJobs

Specify which jobs to keep after finishing. If both age and count are specified, then the jobs kept will be the ones that satisfies both properties.

interface KeepJobs {  
    [age](v5.KeepJobs.html#age)
?: number;  
    [count](v5.KeepJobs.html#count)
?: number;  
}

Properties
----------

### attemptsMade[](#attemptsMade)

attemptsMade: number

Number of attempts after the job has failed.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### data[](#data)

data: [DataType](v5.MinimalJob.html#DataType)

The payload for this job.

### delay[](#delay)

delay: number

An amount of milliseconds to wait until this job can be processed.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### failedReason[](#failedReason)

failedReason: string

Reason for failing.

### `Optional` finishedOn[](#finishedOn)

finishedOn?: number

Timestamp for when the job finished (completed or failed).

### `Optional` id[](#id)

id?: string

### name[](#name)

name: [NameType](v5.MinimalJob.html#NameType)

The name of the Job

### opts[](#opts)

opts: [JobsOptions](../types/v5.JobsOptions.html)

The options object for this job.

### `Optional` parent[](#parent)

parent?: [ParentKeys](v5.ParentKeys.html)

Object that contains parentId (id) and parent queueKey.

### `Optional` parentKey[](#parentKey)

parentKey?: string

Fully qualified key (including the queue prefix) pointing to the parent of this job.

### `Optional` processedOn[](#processedOn)

processedOn?: number

Timestamp for when the job was processed.

### progress[](#progress)

progress: number | object

The progress a job has performed so far.

#### Default Value

    0
    

### `Optional` repeatJobKey[](#repeatJobKey)

repeatJobKey?: string

Base repeat job key.

### returnvalue[](#returnvalue)

returnvalue: [ReturnType](v5.MinimalJob.html#ReturnType)

The value returned by the processor when processing this job.

#### Default Value

    null
    

### stacktrace[](#stacktrace)

stacktrace: string\[\]

Stacktrace for the error (for failed jobs).

#### Default Value

    null
    

### timestamp[](#timestamp)

timestamp: number

Timestamp when the job was created (unless overridden with job options).

Accessors
---------

*   get prefix(): string
*   #### Returns string
    
    the prefix that is used.

*   get queueName(): string
*   #### Returns string
    

### queueQualifiedName[](#queueQualifiedName)

*   get queueQualifiedName(): string
*   #### Returns string
    
    it includes the prefix, the namespace separator :, and queue name.
    
    #### See
    
    [https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html\_node/Qualified-Names.html](https://www.gnu.org/software/gawk/manual/html_node/Qualified-Names.html)

Base Queue options

    [blockingConnection](v5.QueueBaseOptions.html#blockingConnection)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` blockingConnection[](#blockingConnection)

blockingConnection?: boolean

Denotes commands should retry indefinitely.

#### Deprecated

### connection[](#connection)

connection: [ConnectionOptions](../types/v5.ConnectionOptions.html)

Options for connecting to a Redis instance.

### `Optional` prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

Prefix for all queue keys.

### `Optional` skipVersionCheck[](#skipVersionCheck)

skipVersionCheck?: boolean

Avoid version validation to be greater or equal than v5.0.0.

#### Default Value

    false
    

### `Optional` skipWaitingForReady[](#skipWaitingForReady)

skipWaitingForReady?: boolean

Skip waiting for connection ready.

In some instances if you want the queue to fail fast if the connection is not ready you can set this to true. This could be useful for testing and when adding jobs via HTTP endpoints for example.

### `Optional` telemetry[](#telemetry)

telemetry?: [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
<any\>

Telemetry client

### drained[](#drained)

drained: ((id) => void)

Listen to 'drained' event.

This event is triggered when the queue has drained the waiting list. Note that there could still be delayed jobs waiting their timers to expire and this event will still be triggered as long as the waiting list has emptied.

#### Type declaration

*   *   (id): void
    *   Listen to 'drained' event.
        
        This event is triggered when the queue has drained the waiting list. Note that there could still be delayed jobs waiting their timers to expire and this event will still be triggered as long as the waiting list has emptied.
        
        #### Parameters
        
        *   id: string
        
        #### Returns void

# QueueEventsOptions | bullmq - v5.41.8

Interface QueueEventsOptions
============================

Options for QueueEvents

interface QueueEventsOptions {  
    [autorun](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#autorun)
?: boolean;  
    [blockingConnection](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#blockingConnection)
?: boolean;  
    [blockingTimeout](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#blockingTimeout)
?: number;  
    [connection](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#connection)
: [ConnectionOptions](../types/v5.ConnectionOptions.html)
;  
    [lastEventId](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#lastEventId)
?: string;  
    [prefix](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#prefix)
?: string;  
    [skipVersionCheck](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#skipVersionCheck)
?: boolean;  
    [skipWaitingForReady](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#skipWaitingForReady)
?: boolean;  
    [telemetry](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#telemetry)
?: [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
<any\>;  
}

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#v5.QueueEventsOptions)
)

*   [QueueBaseOptions](v5.QueueBaseOptions.html)
    *   QueueEventsOptions

##### Index

### Properties

[autorun?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#autorun)
 [blockingConnection?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#blockingConnection)
 [blockingTimeout?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#blockingTimeout)
 [connection](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#connection)
 [lastEventId?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#lastEventId)
 [prefix?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#prefix)

 [skipWaitingForReady?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#skipWaitingForReady)
 [telemetry?](v5.QueueEventsOptions.html#telemetry)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` autorun[](#autorun)

autorun?: boolean

Condition to start listening to events at instance creation.

### `Optional` blockingConnection[](#blockingConnection)

blockingConnection?: boolean

Denotes commands should retry indefinitely.

#### Deprecated

### `Optional` blockingTimeout[](#blockingTimeout)

blockingTimeout?: number

Timeout for the blocking XREAD call to the events stream.

### connection[](#connection)

connection: [ConnectionOptions](../types/v5.ConnectionOptions.html)

Options for connecting to a Redis instance.

### `Optional` lastEventId[](#lastEventId)

lastEventId?: string

Last event Id. If provided it is possible to continue consuming events from a known Id instead of from the last produced event.

### `Optional` prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

Prefix for all queue keys.

### `Optional` skipVersionCheck[](#skipVersionCheck)

skipVersionCheck?: boolean

Avoid version validation to be greater or equal than v5.0.0.

#### Default Value

    false
    

### `Optional` skipWaitingForReady[](#skipWaitingForReady)

skipWaitingForReady?: boolean

Skip waiting for connection ready.

In some instances if you want the queue to fail fast if the connection is not ready you can set this to true. This could be useful for testing and when adding jobs via HTTP endpoints for example.

### `Optional` telemetry[](#telemetry)

telemetry?: [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
<any\>

Telemetry client

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

Properties
----------

### cleaned[](#cleaned)

cleaned: ((jobs, type) => void)

Listen to 'cleaned' event.

This event is triggered when the queue calls clean method.

----------

### `Optional` blockingConnection[](#blockingConnection)

blockingConnection?: boolean

Denotes commands should retry indefinitely.

#### Deprecated

### connection[](#connection)

connection: [ConnectionOptions](../types/v5.ConnectionOptions.html)

Options for connecting to a Redis instance.

### `Optional` defaultJobOptions[](#defaultJobOptions)

defaultJobOptions?: [DefaultJobOptions](v5.DefaultJobOptions.html)

### `Optional` prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

Prefix for all queue keys.

### `Optional` settings[](#settings)

settings?: [AdvancedRepeatOptions](v5.AdvancedRepeatOptions.html)

Advanced options for the repeatable jobs.

### `Optional` skipMetasUpdate[](#skipMetasUpdate)

skipMetasUpdate?: boolean

Skip Meta update.

If true, the queue will not update the metadata of the queue. Useful for read-only systems that do should not update the metadata.

#### Default Value

    false
    

### `Optional` skipVersionCheck[](#skipVersionCheck)

skipVersionCheck?: boolean

Avoid version validation to be greater or equal than v5.0.0.

#### Default Value

    false
    

### `Optional` skipWaitingForReady[](#skipWaitingForReady)

skipWaitingForReady?: boolean

Skip waiting for connection ready.

In some instances if you want the queue to fail fast if the connection is not ready you can set this to true. This could be useful for testing and when adding jobs via HTTP endpoints for example.

### `Optional` streams[](#streams)

streams?: {  
    events: {  
        maxLen: number;  
    };  
}

Options for the streams used internally in BullMQ.

#### Type declaration

*   ##### events: {  
        maxLen: number;  
    }
    
    Options for the events stream.
    
    *   ##### maxLen: number
        
        Max approximated length for streams. Default is 10 000 events.
        

### `Optional` telemetry[](#telemetry)

telemetry?: [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
<any\>

Telemetry client

Interface RepeatOptions
=======================

Settings for repeatable jobs

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/repeatable](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/jobs/repeatable)

interface RepeatOptions {  
    [count](v5.RepeatOptions.html#count)
?: number;  
    [every](v5.RepeatOptions.html#every)
?: number;  
    [immediately](v5.RepeatOptions.html#immediately)
?: boolean;  
    [jobId](v5.RepeatOptions.html#jobId)
?: string;  
    [key](v5.RepeatOptions.html#key)
?: string;  
    [limit](v5.RepeatOptions.html#limit)
?: number;  
    [offset](v5.RepeatOptions.html#offset)
?: number;  
    [pattern](v5.RepeatOptions.html#pattern)
?: string;  
    [prevMillis](v5.RepeatOptions.html#prevMillis)
?: number;  
}

#### Hierarchy

*   Omit<ParserOptions, "iterator"\>
    *   RepeatOptions

##### Index

### Properties

[count?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#count)
 [every?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#every)
 [immediately?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#immediately)
 [jobId?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#jobId)
 [key?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#key)
 [limit?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#limit)
 [offset?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#offset)
 [pattern?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#pattern)
 [prevMillis?](v5.RepeatOptions.html#prevMillis)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` count[](#count)

count?: number

The start value for the repeat iteration count.

### `Optional` every[](#every)

every?: number

Repeat after this amount of milliseconds (`pattern` setting cannot be used together with this setting.)

### `Optional` immediately[](#immediately)

immediately?: boolean

Repeated job should start right now ( work only with cron settings)

### `Optional` jobId[](#jobId)

jobId?: string

Internal property to store de job id

#### Deprecated

### `Optional` key[](#key)

key?: string

Custom repeatable key. This is the key that holds the "metadata" of a given repeatable job. This key is normally auto-generated but it is sometimes useful to specify a custom key for easier retrieval of repeatable jobs.

### `Optional` limit[](#limit)

limit?: number

Number of times the job should repeat at max.

### `Optional` offset[](#offset)

offset?: number

Offset in milliseconds to affect the next iteration time

### `Optional` pattern[](#pattern)

pattern?: string

A repeat pattern

### `Optional` prevMillis[](#prevMillis)

prevMillis?: number

Internal property to store the previous time the job was executed.

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

interface SandboxedOptions {  
    [useWorkerThreads](v5.SandboxedOptions.html#useWorkerThreads)
?: boolean;  
    [workerForkOptions](v5.SandboxedOptions.html#workerForkOptions)
?: ForkOptions;  
    [workerThreadsOptions](v5.SandboxedOptions.html#workerThreadsOptions)
?: WorkerOptions;

##### Index

### Properties

 [workerThreadsOptions?](v5.SandboxedOptions.html#workerThreadsOptions)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` useWorkerThreads[](#useWorkerThreads)

useWorkerThreads?: boolean

Use Worker Threads instead of Child Processes. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument.

#### Default

    false
    

### `Optional` workerForkOptions[](#workerForkOptions)

workerForkOptions?: ForkOptions

Support passing Worker Fork Options. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument and useWorkerThreads is passed as false (default value).

#### See

[https://nodejs.org/api/child\_process.html#child\_processforkmodulepath-args-options](https://nodejs.org/api/child_process.html#child_processforkmodulepath-args-options)

### `Optional` workerThreadsOptions[](#workerThreadsOptions)

workerThreadsOptions?: WorkerOptions

Support passing Worker Threads Options. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument and useWorkerThreads is passed as true.

#### See

[https://nodejs.org/api/worker\_threads.html#new-workerfilename-options](https://nodejs.org/api/worker_threads.html#new-workerfilename-options)

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

# Telemetry | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
    

Interface Telemetry<Context>
============================

Telemetry interface

This interface allows third-party libraries to integrate their own telemetry system. The interface is heavily inspired by OpenTelemetry but it's not limited to it.

interface Telemetry<[Context](v5.Telemetry.html#Context)
\> {  
    [contextManager](v5.Telemetry.html#contextManager)
: [ContextManager](v5.ContextManager.html)
<any\>;  
    [tracer](v5.Telemetry.html#tracer)
: [Tracer](v5.Tracer.html)
<[Context](v5.Telemetry.html#Context)
\>;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   Context = any

##### Index

### Properties

[contextManager](v5.Telemetry.html#contextManager)
 [tracer](v5.Telemetry.html#tracer)

Properties
----------

### contextManager[](#contextManager)

contextManager: [ContextManager](v5.ContextManager.html)
<any\>

Context manager instance

The context manager is responsible for managing the context and propagating it across the application.

### tracer[](#tracer)

tracer: [Tracer](v5.Tracer.html)
<[Context](v5.Telemetry.html#Context)
\>

Tracer instance

The tracer is responsible for creating spans and propagating the context across the application.

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

##### Index

### Methods

[startSpan](v5.Tracer.html#startSpan)

Methods
-------

### startSpan[](#startSpan)

*   startSpan(name, options?, context?): [Span](v5.Span.html)
    <any\>[](#startSpan.startSpan-1)
    
*   startSpan creates a new Span with the given name and options on an optional context. If the context is not provided, the current active context should be used.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   name: string
    *   `Optional` options: [SpanOptions](v5.SpanOptions.html)
        
    *   `Optional` context: [Context](v5.Tracer.html#Context)
        
    
    #### Returns [Span](v5.Span.html)
    <any\>

drained: (() => void)

Listen to 'drained' event.

This event is triggered when the queue has drained the waiting list. Note that there could still be delayed jobs waiting their timers to expire and this event will still be triggered as long as the waiting list has emptied.

failed: ((job, error, prev) => void)

Properties

### `Optional` autorun[](#autorun)

autorun?: boolean

Condition to start processor at instance creation.

#### Default

    true
    

### `Optional` blockingConnection[](#blockingConnection)

blockingConnection?: boolean

Denotes commands should retry indefinitely.

#### Deprecated

### `Optional` concurrency[](#concurrency)

concurrency?: number

Amount of jobs that a single worker is allowed to work on in parallel.

#### Default

    1
    

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/workers/concurrency](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/workers/concurrency)

### connection[](#connection)

connection: [ConnectionOptions](../types/v5.ConnectionOptions.html)

Options for connecting to a Redis instance.

### `Optional` drainDelay[](#drainDelay)

drainDelay?: number

Number of seconds to long poll for jobs when the queue is empty.

#### Default

    5
    

### `Optional` limiter[](#limiter)

limiter?: [RateLimiterOptions](v5.RateLimiterOptions.html)

Enable rate limiter

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/rate-limiting](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/rate-limiting)

### `Optional` lockDuration[](#lockDuration)

lockDuration?: number

Duration of the lock for the job in milliseconds. The lock represents that a worker is processing the job. If the lock is lost, the job will be eventually be picked up by the stalled checker and move back to wait so that another worker can process it again.

#### Default

    30000
    

### `Optional` lockRenewTime[](#lockRenewTime)

lockRenewTime?: number

The time in milliseconds before the lock is automatically renewed.

It is not recommended to modify this value, which is by default set to halv the lockDuration value, which is optimal for most use cases.

### `Optional` maxStalledCount[](#maxStalledCount)

maxStalledCount?: number

Amount of times a job can be recovered from a stalled state to the `wait` state. If this is exceeded, the job is moved to `failed`.

#### Default

    1
    

### `Optional` metrics[](#metrics)

metrics?: [MetricsOptions](v5.MetricsOptions.html)

Enable collect metrics.

#### See

[https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/metrics](https://docs.bullmq.io/guide/metrics)

### `Optional` name[](#name)

name?: string

Optional worker name. The name will be stored on every job processed by this worker instance, and can be used to monitor which worker is processing or has processed a given job.

### `Optional` prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

Prefix for all queue keys.

### `Optional` removeOnComplete[](#removeOnComplete)

removeOnComplete?: [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

You can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. Default behavior is to keep the job in the completed set.

### `Optional` removeOnFail[](#removeOnFail)

removeOnFail?: [KeepJobs](v5.KeepJobs.html)

You can provide an object specifying max age and/or count to keep. Default behavior is to keep the job in the failed set.

### `Optional` runRetryDelay[](#runRetryDelay)

runRetryDelay?: number

This is an internal option that should not be modified.

#### Default

    15000
    

### `Optional` settings[](#settings)

settings?: [AdvancedOptions](v5.AdvancedOptions.html)

More advanced options.

### `Optional` skipLockRenewal[](#skipLockRenewal)

skipLockRenewal?: boolean

Skip lock renewal for this worker. If set to true, the lock will expire after lockDuration and moved back to the wait queue (if the stalled check is not disabled)

#### Default

    false
    

### `Optional` skipStalledCheck[](#skipStalledCheck)

skipStalledCheck?: boolean

Skip stalled check for this worker. Note that other workers could still perform stalled checkd and move jobs back to wait for jobs being processed by this worker.

#### Default

    false
    

### `Optional` skipVersionCheck[](#skipVersionCheck)

skipVersionCheck?: boolean

Avoid version validation to be greater or equal than v5.0.0.

#### Default Value

    false
    

### `Optional` skipWaitingForReady[](#skipWaitingForReady)

skipWaitingForReady?: boolean

Skip waiting for connection ready.

In some instances if you want the queue to fail fast if the connection is not ready you can set this to true. This could be useful for testing and when adding jobs via HTTP endpoints for example.

### `Optional` stalledInterval[](#stalledInterval)

stalledInterval?: number

Number of milliseconds between stallness checks.

#### Default

    30000
    

### `Optional` telemetry[](#telemetry)

telemetry?: [Telemetry](v5.Telemetry.html)
<any\>

Telemetry Addon

### `Optional` useWorkerThreads[](#useWorkerThreads)

useWorkerThreads?: boolean

Use Worker Threads instead of Child Processes. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument.

#### Default

    false
    

### `Optional` workerForkOptions[](#workerForkOptions)

workerForkOptions?: ForkOptions

Support passing Worker Fork Options. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument and useWorkerThreads is passed as false (default value).

#### See

[https://nodejs.org/api/child\_process.html#child\_processforkmodulepath-args-options](https://nodejs.org/api/child_process.html#child_processforkmodulepath-args-options)

### `Optional` workerThreadsOptions[](#workerThreadsOptions)

workerThreadsOptions?: WorkerOptions

Support passing Worker Threads Options. Note: This option can only be used when specifying a file for the processor argument and useWorkerThreads is passed as true.

#### See

[https://nodejs.org/api/worker\_threads.html#new-workerfilename-options](https://nodejs.org/api/worker_threads.html#new-workerfilename-options)

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

# CompressableJobOptions | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [CompressableJobOptions](v5.CompressableJobOptions.html)
    

Type alias CompressableJobOptions
=================================

CompressableJobOptions: {  
    debounce?: [DebounceOptions](../interfaces/v5.DebounceOptions.html)
;  
    deduplication?: [DebounceOptions](../interfaces/v5.DebounceOptions.html)
;  
    failParentOnFailure?: boolean;  
    ignoreDependencyOnFailure?: boolean;  
    removeDependencyOnFailure?: boolean;  
    telemetry?: {  
        metadata?: string;  
        omitContext?: boolean;  
    };  
}

These options will be stored in Redis with smaller keys for compactness.

#### Type declaration

*   ##### `Optional` debounce?: [DebounceOptions](../interfaces/v5.DebounceOptions.html)
    
    Debounce options.
    
    #### Deprecated
    
    use deduplication option
    
*   ##### `Optional` deduplication?: [DebounceOptions](../interfaces/v5.DebounceOptions.html)
    
    Deduplication options.
    
*   ##### `Optional` failParentOnFailure?: boolean
    
    If true, moves parent to failed.
    
*   ##### `Optional` ignoreDependencyOnFailure?: boolean
    
    If true, moves the jobId from its parent dependencies to failed dependencies when it fails after all attempts.
    
*   ##### `Optional` removeDependencyOnFailure?: boolean
    
    If true, removes the job from its parent dependencies when it fails after all attempts.
    
*   ##### `Optional` telemetry?: {  
        metadata?: string;  
        omitContext?: boolean;  
    }
    
    Telemetry options
    
    *   ##### `Optional` metadata?: string
        
        Metadata, used for context propagation.
        
    *   ##### `Optional` omitContext?: boolean
        
        If `true` telemetry will omit the context propagation
        
        #### Default
        
            false
            
        

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark

Generated using [TypeDoc](https://typedoc.org/)

# RedisJobOptions | bullmq - v5.41.8

*   [bullmq](../index.html)
    
*   [v5](../modules/v5.html)
    
*   [RedisJobOptions](v5.RedisJobOptions.html)
    

Type alias RedisJobOptions
==========================

RedisJobOptions: [BaseJobOptions](../interfaces/v5.BaseJobOptions.html)
 & {  
    de?: string;  
    deid?: string;  
    fpof?: boolean;  
    idof?: boolean;  
    kl?: number;  
    omc?: boolean;  
    rdof?: boolean;  
    tm?: string;  
}

These fields are the ones stored in Redis with smaller keys for compactness.

#### Type declaration

*   ##### `Optional` de?: string
    
    Deduplication identifier.
    
    #### Deprecated
    
    use deid
    
*   ##### `Optional` deid?: string
    
    Debounce identifier.
    
*   ##### `Optional` fpof?: boolean
    
    If true, moves parent to failed.
    
*   ##### `Optional` idof?: boolean
    
    If true, moves the jobId from its parent dependencies to failed dependencies when it fails after all attempts.
    
*   ##### `Optional` kl?: number
    
    Maximum amount of log entries that will be preserved
    
*   ##### `Optional` omc?: boolean
    
    Omit Context Propagation
    
*   ##### `Optional` rdof?: boolean
    
    If true, removes the job from its parent dependencies when it fails after all attempts.
    
*   ##### `Optional` tm?: string
    
    TelemetryMetadata, provide for context propagation.
    

### Settings

#### Member Visibility

*   Inherited

#### Theme

OSLightDark
